Nested regions are\n * supported; unmatched start or end markers are ignored.\n */\nexport function getNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): NamedRegion[] {\n\tconst results: NamedRegion[] = [];\n\tconst stack: { name: string; startLineNumber: number }[] = [];\n\n\tfor (let line = 1; line <= model.getLineCount(); line++) {\n\t\tconst lineContent = model.getLineContent(line);\n\n\t\tconst startMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_START_PATTERN);\n\t\tif (startMatch) {\n\t\t\tstack.push({ name: startMatch[1], startLineNumber: line });\n\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tconst endMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_END_PATTERN);\n\t\tif (endMatch && stack.length > 0) {\n\t\t\tconst region = stack.pop()!;\n\t\t\tresults.push({\n\t\t\t\tname: region.name,\n\t\t\t\tstartLineNumber: region.startLineNumber,\n\t\t\t\tendLineNumber: line,\n\t\t\t});\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Sort by start line so callers get a predictable order\n\tresults.sort((a, b) => a.startLineNumber - b.startLineNumber);\n\treturn results;\n}\n\n/**\n * Build a map from region name to the first matching NamedRegion.\n * If two regions share the same name the one with the smaller start line wins.\n */\nexport function buildNamedRegionMap(regions: NamedRegion[]): Map<string, NamedRegion> {\n\tconst map = new Map<string, NamedRegion>();\n\tfor (const region of regions) {\n\t\tif (!map.has(region.name)) {\n\t\t\tmap.set(region.name, region);\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn map;\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":160,"cache_read_input_tokens":64301,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":160,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":24,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d6722c7a-6677-469d-aa0d-c5019541b45b","uuid":"b5e299eb-f46b-424b-9706-3bb4d5762ec7"}
